The extension pauses all sort of window opening requests for user attention. You can either accept or deny a request. Multiple unique requests are shown in an array. If a websites requests a single URL more than once, a badge number will be shown indicating the total number of requests to this particular URL.\r\n\r\n\r\nPlease note that the extension is recently renamed from \"Popup Blocker (ultimate)\" to \"Popup Blocker (strict)\"\r\n\r\nOptions:\r\n1. Deny popup request\r\n2. Allow popup request\r\n3. Open popup request in a background tab\r\n4. Redirect current page to popup URL source\r\n\r\nSupported blocking methods:\r\n1. window.open\r\n2. a->target=_blank\r\n\r\nFor bug reports please go to:\r\nhttps://github.com/schomery/popup-blocker/issues\r\n\r\nFor FAQs please go to:\r\nhttp://add0n.com/popup-blocker.html\r\n\r\nFor testing your current popup blocker effectiveness go
